2. Tech stack summary
Languages:
- TypeScript (root runtime + Next.js app)
- JavaScript (compiled output under dist/)
- SQL (SQLite schema/migrations in code strings)
- Shell (scripts/pi/*.sh)
Frameworks/Runtimes:
- Node.js runtime (npm scripts + tsx + node)
- Next.js 14.2.35 (apps/mission-control/package.json)
- React 18.2.0 (apps/mission-control/package.json)
- Tailwind CSS 3.4.17 (apps/mission-control/package.json)
Core libraries (root):
{
  "name": "openclaw-local-agent-mvp",
  "version": "0.1.0",
  "private": true,
  "description": "Single-node local voice-orchestrated multi-agent MVP scaffold",
  "scripts": {
    "build": "tsc -p tsconfig.json",
    "typecheck": "tsc --noEmit -p tsconfig.json",
    "start": "node dist/index.js",
    "dev": "tsx src/index.ts",
    "mc:install": "npm --prefix apps/mission-control install",
    "mc:dev": "npm --prefix apps/mission-control run dev",
    "mc:dev:safe": "npm --prefix apps/mission-control run dev:safe",
    "mc:build": "npm --prefix apps/mission-control run build",
    "mc:start": "npm --prefix apps/mission-control run start",
    "mc:start:safe": "npm --prefix apps/mission-control run start:safe",
    "test": "npm run build && node --test dist/tests/**/*.test.js",

3. Entry points
- src/index.ts: Main runtime bootstrap that chooses mode (local/openclaw/openclaw-bridge/mission-control), wires stores, orchestrator, scheduler, telephony, and starts the selected server/adapter.
- src/missionControl/server.ts: HTTP Mission Control backend server exposing dashboard and orchestration/task/pipeline APIs in non-Next runtime mode.
- src/openclaw/bridgeServer.ts: OpenClaw bridge HTTP/WebSocket server for inbound events, realtime session brokerage, voice lab, and telephony endpoints.
- apps/mission-control/src/app/layout.tsx: Next.js root layout entry for the Mission Control web app shell and global styling.
- apps/mission-control/src/app/page.tsx: Next.js landing page entry listing/creating workspaces and routing into workspace dashboards.
- apps/mission-control/src/app/workspace/[slug]/page.tsx: Main workspace dashboard entry rendering agents, queue, planner, and live feed with polling/SSE hooks.

4. Existing services & integrations
- OpenClaw Gateway (WebSocket RPC): apps/mission-control/src/lib/openclaw/client.ts and src/openclaw/inboundAdapter.ts connect via ws/wss and call methods like chat.send/sessions.*.
- OpenAI Chat Completions (REST HTTPS): src/models/provider.ts and apps/mission-control/src/lib/mission-planner.ts call /v1/chat/completions.
- OpenAI Realtime Sessions (REST HTTPS): src/openclaw/realtimeSessionBroker.ts posts to /v1/realtime/sessions.
- OpenRouter (OpenAI-compatible REST HTTPS): src/models/provider.ts uses OPENROUTER_BASE_URL with OpenAI-compatible payloads + HTTP-Referer/X-Title headers.
- Twilio Voice API (REST HTTPS + Webhooks): src/telephony/twilioDialer.ts posts to Twilio Calls API; src/openclaw/bridgeServer.ts serves /twilio/voice, /twilio/status, /twilio/media, /twilio/gather.
- Social dispatch webhooks (REST HTTP POST): src/pipeline/postDispatch.ts sends queued payloads to TIKTOK_DISPATCH_WEBHOOK / REELS_DISPATCH_WEBHOOK / SHORTS_DISPATCH_WEBHOOK.
- Agent completion webhook (internal REST): apps/mission-control/src/app/api/webhooks/agent-completion/route.ts receives completion callbacks.
- Google Fonts CDN (HTTP GET): apps/mission-control/src/app/layout.tsx loads JetBrains Mono from fonts.googleapis.com.
- Mission Control internal service-to-service HTTP: apps/mission-control task routes trigger internal /dispatch endpoints and status APIs via localhost URL construction.

5. Database & state
Datastores/files:
- SQLite (root runtime): default DB_PATH data/mvp.sqlite (src/index.ts).
- SQLite (Next app): apps/mission-control/mission-control.db (apps/mission-control/src/lib/db/index.ts).
- Root placeholder DB file: ./mission-control.db.
- Trace files: ./traces/*.trace.json and *.events.jsonl.
- Test state dirs: ./data-test, ./traces-test.
Schema/model sources:
- src/storage/sqliteTaskStore.ts (tasks table for orchestrator runtime).
- src/trace/sqliteTraceStore.ts (traces + trace_timeline tables).
- src/transcript/sqliteSessionTranscriptStore.ts (session transcripts).
- src/notifications/sqliteNotificationStore.ts (notification queue/persistence).
- src/pipeline/sqlitePipelineStore.ts (pipeline_definitions, runs, nodes, queue, media_jobs, spend ledger, source registry).
- apps/mission-control/src/lib/db/schema.ts (Next app schema).
- apps/mission-control/src/lib/db/migrations.ts (Next app migrations 001..006).
- apps/mission-control/src/lib/db/seed.ts (seed data).

6. Scheduling & automation
- Pipeline scheduler loop: src/pipeline/scheduler.ts uses setInterval (SCHEDULER_TICK_MS, default 60000ms) and starts due runs.
- RRULE-like run progression: src/pipeline/sqlitePipelineStore.ts computeNextRunAt parses INTERVAL=n and advances next_run_at.
- Default pipeline cadence: src/pipeline/engine.ts default definition uses FREQ=HOURLY;INTERVAL=1.
- OpenClaw reconnect automation: apps/mission-control/src/lib/openclaw/client.ts schedules reconnect every 10s when disconnected.
- Mission Control UI polling timers: workspace/header/sidebar/activity components use setInterval for events/tasks/status/subagent counts.
- SSE keepalive automation: apps/mission-control/src/app/api/events/stream/route.ts emits periodic keepalive events.
- Dispatch heartbeat loop: apps/mission-control/src/app/api/tasks/[id]/dispatch/route.ts logs heartbeat activity every 30s while waiting for agent.wait.
- Pi ops automation scripts: scripts/pi/mc-start.sh and scripts/pi/mc-stop.sh for service startup/shutdown.

8. What is clearly missing or incomplete
- Broken script reference: apps/mission-control/package.json defines db:migrate -> tsx src/lib/db/migrate.ts, but src/lib/db/migrate.ts does not exist (directory listing only has index.ts, migrations.ts, schema.ts, seed.ts).
- Telegram integration appears planned but not implemented in this code tree: OPERATIONS/TELEGRAM_CONTROL_PLAN.md specifies endpoints/utilities (e.g., /api/integrations/telegram/webhook, lib/telegram.ts) that are not present.
- Brave Search integration is not present in code (no BRAVE_* env usage), so autonomous trend/news fetching via Brave API is currently not implemented here.
- Several roadmap/operations docs describe future items (OAuth/native publisher adapters, broader mission-control hardening) that are design-level and not fully backed by concrete routes/modules yet.
- There are local binary/state artifacts committed in workspace context (e.g., mission-control.db, .next build output) that can cause environment drift between machines if treated as source-of-truth.
